__kernel void pack_nchw_to_nchwc4(__global Ti* in, __global To* out, const int align_wh, const int width,
const int height, const int chanel, const int offset_in, const int offset_out, int zp,
float scale, int batch, int in_batch_offset, int out_batch_offset)
const int idh  = get_global_id(0);
const int idw  = get_global_id(1);
const int idnc = get_global_id(2);
int idc      = idnc / batch;
int batch_id = idnc % batch;
if ((idw >= ((width + 4) >> 2)) || idh >= height) {
return;
int  in_off  = ((idc << 2) * height + idh) * width + (idw << 2) + offset_in + batch_id * in_batch_offset;
int  out_off = idc * align_wh + idh * width + (idw << 2) + batch_id * out_batch_offset;
char iex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
char oex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
int out_str = 1;
short iec = ((idc << 2) + 4 <= chanel) ? 4 : (chanel & 3);
Ti4 val[4];
int i;
for (i = 0; i < 4; ++i) {
val[i] = 0;
int iwh_str = width * height;
if (iex == 4) {
val[0] = vload4(0, in + in_off);
if (iec > 1) {
val[1] = vload4(0, in + in_off + iwh_str);
if (iec > 2) {
val[2] = vload4(0, in + in_off + (iwh_str << 1));
if (iec > 3) {
val[3] = vload4(0, in + in_off + iwh_str * 3);
} else {
if (iex == 1) {
val[0].x = in[in_off];
if (iec > 1) {
val[1].x = in[in_off + iwh_str];
if (iec > 2) {
val[2].x = in[in_off + (iwh_str << 1)];
if (iec > 3) {
val[3].x = in[in_off + iwh_str * 3];
if (iex == 2) {
val[0].xy = vload2(0, in + in_off);
if (iec > 1) {
val[1].xy = vload2(0, in + in_off + iwh_str);
if (iec > 2) {
val[2].xy = vload2(0, in + in_off + (iwh_str << 1));
if (iec > 3) {
val[3].xy = vload2(0, in + in_off + iwh_str * 3);
if (iex == 3) {
val[0].xyz = vload3(0, in + in_off);
if (iec > 1) {
val[1].xyz = vload3(0, in + in_off + iwh_str);
if (iec > 2) {
val[2].xyz = vload3(0, in + in_off + (iwh_str << 1));
if (iec > 3) {
val[3].xyz = vload3(0, in + in_off + iwh_str * 3);
vstore4((To4)(val[0].x, val[1].x, val[2].x, val[3].x), out_off, out + offset_out);
if (oex > 1) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].y, val[1].y, val[2].y, val[3].y), out_off + out_str, out + offset_out);
if (oex > 2) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].z, val[1].z, val[2].z, val[3].z), out_off + (out_str << 1), out + offset_out);
if (oex > 3) {

int zp, float scale, int batch, int in_batch_offset, int out_batch_offset)

const int idw = get_global_id(1);
const int idc = get_global_id(2);

return;

int  out_off = idc * align_wh + idh * width + (idw << 2);
char iex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
char oex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
int out_str = 1;
short iec = ((idc << 4) + 16 <= chanel) ? 16 : (chanel & 15);
Ti4 val[16];
int i;
for (i = 0; i < 16; ++i) {
val[i] = 0;
int iwh_str = width * height;
if (iex == 4) {
for (i = 0; i < iec; i++) {
val[i] = vload4(0, in + in_off + iwh_str * i);
} else {
if (iex == 1) {
for (i = 0; i < iec; i++) {
val[i].x = in[in_off + iwh_str * i];
if (iex == 2) {
for (i = 0; i < iec; i++) {
val[i].xy = vload2(0, in + in_off + iwh_str * i);
if (iex == 3) {
for (i = 0; i < iec; i++) {
val[i].xyz = vload3(0, in + in_off + iwh_str * i);
vstore16((To16)(val[0].x, val[1].x, val[2].x, val[3].x, val[4].x, val[5].x, val[6].x, val[7].x, val[8].x, val[9].x,
val[10].x, val[11].x, val[12].x, val[13].x, val[14].x, val[15].x),
out_off, out + offset_out);
if (oex > 1) {
vstore16((To16)(val[0].y, val[1].y, val[2].y, val[3].y, val[4].y, val[5].y, val[6].y, val[7].y, val[8].y, val[9].y,
val[10].y, val[11].y, val[12].y, val[13].y, val[14].y, val[15].y),
out_off + out_str, out + offset_out);
if (oex > 2) {
vstore16((To16)(val[0].z, val[1].z, val[2].z, val[3].z, val[4].z, val[5].z, val[6].z, val[7].z, val[8].z, val[9].z,
val[10].z, val[11].z, val[12].z, val[13].z, val[14].z, val[15].z),
out_off + (out_str << 1), out + offset_out);
if (oex > 3) {
vstore16((To16)(val[0].w, val[1].w, val[2].w, val[3].w, val[4].w, val[5].w, val[6].w, val[7].w, val[8].w, val[9].w,
val[10].w, val[11].w, val[12].w, val[13].w, val[14].w, val[15].w),
out_off + out_str * 3, out + offset_out);
__kernel void pack_nchw_to_nchwc16_quant(__global Ti* in, __global To* out, const int align_wh, const int width,
const int height, const int chanel, const int offset_in, const int offset_out,
int zp, float scale)
const int idh = get_global_id(0);
const int idw = get_global_id(1);
const int idc = get_global_id(2);
if ((idw >= ((width + 3) >> 2)) || idh >= height || (idc >= ((chanel + 15) >> 4))) {
return;
int  in_off  = ((idc << 4) * height + idh) * width + (idw << 2) + offset_in;
int  out_off = idc * align_wh + idh * width + (idw << 2);
char iex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
char oex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
short iec = ((idc << 4) + 16 <= chanel) ? 16 : (chanel & 15);
Ti4 val[16];
int i;
for (i = 0; i < 16; ++i) {
val[i] = 0;
int iwh_str = width * height;
if (iex == 4) {
for (i = 0; i < iec; i++) {
val[i] = vload4(0, in + in_off + iwh_str * i);
} else {
if (iex == 1) {
for (i = 0; i < iec; i++) {
val[i].x = in[in_off + iwh_str * i];
if (iex == 2) {
for (i = 0; i < iec; i++) {
val[i].xy = vload2(0, in + in_off + iwh_str * i);
if (iex == 3) {
for (i = 0; i < iec; i++) {
val[i].xyz = vload3(0, in + in_off + iwh_str * i);
for (i = 0; i < 16; i++) {
val[i].x = clamp((Ti)round(val[i].x / scale + zp), (Ti)-128, (Ti)127);
val[i].y = clamp((Ti)round(val[i].y / scale + zp), (Ti)-128, (Ti)127);
val[i].z = clamp((Ti)round(val[i].z / scale + zp), (Ti)-128, (Ti)127);
val[i].w = clamp((Ti)round(val[i].w / scale + zp), (Ti)-128, (Ti)127);
vstore16((To16)(val[0].x, val[1].x, val[2].x, val[3].x, val[4].x, val[5].x, val[6].x, val[7].x, val[8].x, val[9].x,
val[10].x, val[11].x, val[12].x, val[13].x, val[14].x, val[15].x),
out_off, out + offset_out);
if (oex > 1) {
vstore16((To16)(val[0].y, val[1].y, val[2].y, val[3].y, val[4].y, val[5].y, val[6].y, val[7].y, val[8].y, val[9].y,
val[10].y, val[11].y, val[12].y, val[13].y, val[14].y, val[15].y),
out_off + 1, out + offset_out);
if (oex > 2) {
vstore16((To16)(val[0].z, val[1].z, val[2].z, val[3].z, val[4].z, val[5].z, val[6].z, val[7].z, val[8].z, val[9].z,
val[10].z, val[11].z, val[12].z, val[13].z, val[14].z, val[15].z),
out_off + 2, out + offset_out);
if (oex > 3) {
vstore16((To16)(val[0].w, val[1].w, val[2].w, val[3].w, val[4].w, val[5].w, val[6].w, val[7].w, val[8].w, val[9].w,
val[10].w, val[11].w, val[12].w, val[13].w, val[14].w, val[15].w),
out_off + 3, out + offset_out);

const unsigned int elems)

if (gid < elems) {
float in_value           = input[in_offset + gid];
output[out_offset + gid] = in_value >= 0.f ? in_value : 0.f;

__kernel void unpack_nchwc16_to_nchw(__global Ti* in, __global To* out, const int align_wh, const int width,
const int height, const int chanel, const int offset_in, const int offset_out,
int zp, float scale, int batch, int in_batch_offset, int out_batch_offset)
const int idh  = get_global_id(0);
const int idw  = get_global_id(1);
const int idnc = get_global_id(2);
int idc      = idnc / batch;
int batch_id = idnc % batch;
if ((idw >= ((width + 3) >> 2)) || idh >= height || (idc >= ((chanel + 15) >> 4))) {
return;
int  in_off  = idc * align_wh + idh * width + (idw << 2) + batch_id * in_batch_offset;
int  out_off = ((idc << 4) * height + idh) * width + (idw << 2) + offset_out + batch_id * out_batch_offset;
char iex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
char oex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
const int in_str = 1;
short oec = ((idc << 4) + 16 <= chanel) ? 16 : (chanel & 15);
Ti16 val[4];
int  i;
for (i = 0; i < 4; ++i) {
val[i] = 0;
if (iex > 0) {
val[0] = vload16(in_off, in + offset_in);
if (iex > 1) {
val[1] = vload16(in_off + in_str, in + offset_in);
if (iex > 2) {
val[2] = vload16(in_off + (in_str << 1), in + offset_in);
if (iex > 3) {

if (oec > 1) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].s1, val[1].s1, val[2].s1, val[3].s1), 0, out + out_off + owh_str);
if (oec > 2) {

if (oec > 3) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].s3, val[1].s3, val[2].s3, val[3].s3), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 3);
if (oec > 4) {

if (oec > 9) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].s9, val[1].s9, val[2].s9, val[3].s9), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 9);

if (oec > 13) {

if (oec > 15) {

} else {

__kernel void unpack_nchwc16_to_nchw_dequant(__global Ti* in, __global To* out, const int align_wh, const int width,
const int height, const int chanel, const int offset_in,
const int offset_out, int zp, float scale, int batch, int in_batch_offset,
int out_batch_offset)
const int idh = get_global_id(0);
const int idw = get_global_id(1);
const int idc = get_global_id(2);
if (((idw >= (width + 3)) >> 2) || idh >= height || (idc >= ((chanel + 15) >> 4))) {
return;
int  in_off  = idc * align_wh + idh * width + (idw << 2);
int  out_off = ((idc << 4) * height + idh) * width + (idw << 2) + offset_out;
char iex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
char oex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
const int in_str = 1;
short oec = ((idc << 4) + 16 <= chanel) ? 16 : (chanel & 15);
Ti16  ival;
To8 val[8];
int i;
for (i = 0; i < i; ++i) {
val[i] = 0;
if (iex > 0) {
ival   = vload16(in_off, in + offset_in);
val[0] = (To8)((ival.s0 - zp) * scale, (ival.s1 - zp) * scale, (ival.s2 - zp) * scale, (ival.s3 - zp) * scale,
(ival.s4 - zp) * scale, (ival.s5 - zp) * scale, (ival.s6 - zp) * scale, (ival.s7 - zp) * scale);
val[4] = (To8)((ival.s8 - zp) * scale, (ival.s9 - zp) * scale, (ival.sa - zp) * scale, (ival.sb - zp) * scale,
(ival.sc - zp) * scale, (ival.sd - zp) * scale, (ival.se - zp) * scale, (ival.sf - zp) * scale);
if (iex > 1) {
ival   = vload16(in_off + in_str, in + offset_in);
val[1] = (To8)((ival.s0 - zp) * scale, (ival.s1 - zp) * scale, (ival.s2 - zp) * scale, (ival.s3 - zp) * scale,
(ival.s4 - zp) * scale, (ival.s5 - zp) * scale, (ival.s6 - zp) * scale, (ival.s7 - zp) * scale);
val[5] = (To8)((ival.s8 - zp) * scale, (ival.s9 - zp) * scale, (ival.sa - zp) * scale, (ival.sb - zp) * scale,
(ival.sc - zp) * scale, (ival.sd - zp) * scale, (ival.se - zp) * scale, (ival.sf - zp) * scale);
if (iex > 2) {
ival   = vload16(in_off + (in_str << 1), in + offset_in);
val[2] = (To8)((ival.s0 - zp) * scale, (ival.s1 - zp) * scale, (ival.s2 - zp) * scale, (ival.s3 - zp) * scale,
(ival.s4 - zp) * scale, (ival.s5 - zp) * scale, (ival.s6 - zp) * scale, (ival.s7 - zp) * scale);

(ival.sc - zp) * scale, (ival.sd - zp) * scale, (ival.se - zp) * scale, (ival.sf - zp) * scale);
if (iex > 3) {
ival   = vload16(in_off + in_str * 3, in + offset_in);
val[3] = (To8)((ival.s0 - zp) * scale, (ival.s1 - zp) * scale, (ival.s2 - zp) * scale, (ival.s3 - zp) * scale,
(ival.s4 - zp) * scale, (ival.s5 - zp) * scale, (ival.s6 - zp) * scale, (ival.s7 - zp) * scale);

(ival.sc - zp) * scale, (ival.sd - zp) * scale, (ival.se - zp) * scale, (ival.sf - zp) * scale);

vstore3((To3)(val[4].s7, val[5].s7, val[6].s7), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 15);
#pragma OPENCL EXTENSION cl_khr_fp16 : enable
#define GLOBAL_SIZE_2_DIMS __private const int global_size_dim0, __private const int global_size_dim1,__private const int global_size_dim2,
#define DEAL_NON_UNIFORM_DIM2(input1, input2,input3)                     \
if (input1 >= global_size_dim0 || input2 >= global_size_dim1 || input3 >= global_size_dim2) { \
return;                                                       \
__kernel void matmul_buf(GLOBAL_SIZE_2_DIMS __global const T* input_a, __global const T* input_b, __global T* output_c,
__private const int in_a_offset,__private const int in_b_offset,__private const int out_c_offset,
__private const int M,__private const int K, __private const int N, __private const int K_blocks,
__private const int N_blocks)
const int C_idx        = get_global_id(0);
const int N_blocks_idx = get_global_id(1);
const int M_idx        = get_global_id(2);
DEAL_NON_UNIFORM_DIM2(C_idx, N_blocks_idx, M_idx);
int out_remain = (N_blocks_idx + 1) * 4 - N;
T4 a;
T4 b0 = 0, b1 = 0, b2 = 0, b3 = 0;
T4 btmp0 = 0, btmp1 = 0, btmp2 = 0, btmp3 = 0;
T result0 = 0;
T result1 = 0;
T result2 = 0;
T result3 = 0;
for (short pos = 0; pos < K_blocks; pos += 1) {
const int inpa_offset = M_idx * K + pos * 4 + M * K * C_idx + in_a_offset;
short remain = (pos + 1) * 4 - K;
if (remain == 1) {
T3 a_ = vload3(0, input_a + inpa_offset);
a = (T4)(a_.s0, a_.s1, a_.s2, 0);
} else if (remain == 2) {
T2 a_ = vload2(0, input_a + inpa_offset);
a = (T4)(a_.s0, a_.s1, 0, 0);
} else if (remain == 3) {
T a_ = input_a[inpa_offset];
a = (T4)(a_, 0, 0, 0);
} else {
a = vload4(0, input_a + inpa_offset);
const int inpb_offset = pos * N * 4 + N_blocks_idx * 4 + K * N * C_idx + in_b_offset;
if(out_remain == 1){
if (remain == 1) {
T3 b0_temp = vload3(0, input_b + inpb_offset);
T3 b1_temp = vload3(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N);
T3 b2_temp = vload3(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N * 2);
b0 = (T4)(b0_temp.s0, b0_temp.s1, b0_temp.s2, 0);
b1 = (T4)(b1_temp.s0, b1_temp.s1, b1_temp.s2, 0);
b2 = (T4)(b2_temp.s0, b2_temp.s1, b2_temp.s2, 0);
b3 = 0;
} else if (remain == 2) {
T3 b0_temp = vload3(0, input_b + inpb_offset);
T3 b1_temp = vload3(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N);
b0 = (T4)(b0_temp.s0, b0_temp.s1, b0_temp.s2, 0);
b1 = (T4)(b1_temp.s0, b1_temp.s1, b1_temp.s2, 0);
b2 = 0;
b3 = 0;
} else if (remain == 3) {
T3 b0_temp = vload3(0, input_b + inpb_offset);
b0 = (T4)(b0_temp.s0, b0_temp.s1, b0_temp.s2, 0);
b1 = 0;
b2 = 0;
b3 = 0;
} else {
T3 b0_temp = vload3(0, input_b + inpb_offset);
T3 b1_temp = vload3(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N);
T3 b2_temp = vload3(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N * 2);
T3 b3_temp = vload3(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N * 3);
b0 = (T4)(b0_temp.s0, b0_temp.s1, b0_temp.s2, 0);
b1 = (T4)(b1_temp.s0, b1_temp.s1, b1_temp.s2, 0);
b2 = (T4)(b2_temp.s0, b2_temp.s1, b2_temp.s2, 0);
b3 = (T4)(b3_temp.s0, b3_temp.s1, b3_temp.s2, 0);
}else if(out_remain == 2){
if (remain == 1) {
T2 b0_temp = vload2(0, input_b + inpb_offset);
T2 b1_temp = vload2(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N);
T2 b2_temp = vload2(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N * 2);
b0 = (T4)(b0_temp.s0, b0_temp.s1, 0, 0);
b1 = (T4)(b1_temp.s0, b1_temp.s1, 0, 0);
b2 = (T4)(b2_temp.s0, b2_temp.s1, 0, 0);
b3 = 0;
} else if (remain == 2) {
T2 b0_temp = vload2(0, input_b + inpb_offset);
T2 b1_temp = vload2(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N);
b0 = (T4)(b0_temp.s0, b0_temp.s1, 0, 0);
b1 = (T4)(b1_temp.s0, b1_temp.s1, 0, 0);
b2 = 0;
b3 = 0;
} else if (remain == 3) {

b0 = (T4)(b0_temp.s0, b0_temp.s1, 0, 0);
b1 = 0;
b2 = 0;
b3 = 0;
} else {
T2 b0_temp = vload2(0, input_b + inpb_offset);
T2 b1_temp = vload2(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N);
T2 b2_temp = vload2(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N * 2);
T2 b3_temp = vload2(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N * 3);
b0 = (T4)(b0_temp.s0, b0_temp.s1, 0, 0);
b1 = (T4)(b1_temp.s0, b1_temp.s1, 0, 0);
b2 = (T4)(b2_temp.s0, b2_temp.s1, 0, 0);
b3 = (T4)(b3_temp.s0, b3_temp.s1, 0, 0);
}else if(out_remain == 3){
if (remain == 1) {
T b0_temp = input_b[inpb_offset];
T b1_temp = input_b[inpb_offset + N];
T b2_temp = input_b[inpb_offset + N * 2];
b0 = (T4)(b0_temp, 0, 0, 0);
b1 = (T4)(b1_temp, 0, 0, 0);
b2 = (T4)(b2_temp, 0, 0, 0);
b3 = 0;
} else if (remain == 2) {
T b0_temp = input_b[inpb_offset];
T b1_temp = input_b[inpb_offset + N];
b0 = (T4)(b0_temp, 0, 0, 0);
b1 = (T4)(b1_temp, 0, 0, 0);
b2 = 0;
b3 = 0;
} else if (remain == 3) {
T b0_temp = input_b[inpb_offset];
b0 = (T4)(b0_temp, 0, 0, 0);
b1 = 0;
b2 = 0;
b3 = 0;
} else {
T b0_temp = input_b[inpb_offset];
T b1_temp = input_b[inpb_offset + N];
T b2_temp = input_b[inpb_offset + N * 2];
T b3_temp = input_b[inpb_offset + N * 3];
b0 = (T4)(b0_temp, 0, 0, 0);
b1 = (T4)(b1_temp, 0, 0, 0);
b2 = (T4)(b2_temp, 0, 0, 0);
b3 = (T4)(b3_temp, 0, 0, 0);

if (remain == 1) {
b0 = vload4(0, input_b + inpb_offset);
b1 = vload4(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N);
b2 = vload4(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N * 2);
b3 = 0;
} else if (remain == 2) {
b0 = vload4(0, input_b + inpb_offset);
b1 = vload4(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N);
b2 = 0;
b3 = 0;
} else if (remain == 3) {
b0 = vload4(0, input_b + inpb_offset);
b1 = 0;
b2 = 0;
b3 = 0;
} else {
b0 = vload4(0, input_b + inpb_offset);
b1 = vload4(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N);
b2 = vload4(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N * 2);
b3 = vload4(0, input_b + inpb_offset + N * 3);
if(out_remain == 1){
btmp0 = (T4)(b0.s0, b1.s0, b2.s0, b3.s0);
btmp1 = (T4)(b0.s1, b1.s1, b2.s1, b3.s1);
btmp2 = (T4)(b0.s2, b1.s2, b2.s2, b3.s2);
result0 += dot(a, btmp0);
result1 += dot(a, btmp1);
result2 += dot(a, btmp2);
}else if(out_remain == 2){
btmp0 = (T4)(b0.s0, b1.s0, b2.s0, b3.s0);
btmp1 = (T4)(b0.s1, b1.s1, b2.s1, b3.s1);
result0 += dot(a, btmp0);
result1 += dot(a, btmp1);
}else if(out_remain == 3){
btmp0 = (T4)(b0.s0, b1.s0, b2.s0, b3.s0);
result0 += dot(a, btmp0);
}else{
btmp0 = (T4)(b0.s0, b1.s0, b2.s0, b3.s0);
btmp1 = (T4)(b0.s1, b1.s1, b2.s1, b3.s1);
btmp2 = (T4)(b0.s2, b1.s2, b2.s2, b3.s2);
btmp3 = (T4)(b0.s3, b1.s3, b2.s3, b3.s3);
result0 += dot(a, btmp0);
result1 += dot(a, btmp1);
result2 += dot(a, btmp2);
result3 += dot(a, btmp3);
const int out_offset = M_idx * N + N_blocks_idx * 4 + M * N * C_idx + out_c_offset;
if(out_remain == 3){
output_c[out_offset] = result0;
}else if(out_remain == 2){
vstore2((T2)(result0, result1), 0, output_c + out_offset);
}else if(out_remain == 1){
vstore3((T3)(result0, result1, result2), 0, output_c + out_offset);
}else{
vstore4((T4)(result0, result1, result2, result3), 0, output_c + out_offset);

#pragma OPENCL EXTENSION cl_khr_fp16 : enable
__kernel void unpack_nchwc4_to_nchw(__global Ti* in, __global To* out, const int align_wh, const int width,
const int height, const int chanel, const int offset_in, const int offset_out,
int zp, float scale, int batch, int in_batch_offset, int out_batch_offset)
const int idh  = get_global_id(0);
const int idw  = get_global_id(1);
const int idnc = get_global_id(2);
int idc      = idnc / batch;
int batch_id = idnc % batch;
if (idh >= height || ((idw << 2) >= width) || (idc >= ((chanel + 3) >> 2))) {
return;
int  in_off  = idc * align_wh + idh * width + (idw << 2) + batch_id * in_batch_offset;
int  out_off = ((idc << 2) * height + idh) * width + (idw << 2) + offset_out + batch_id * out_batch_offset;
char iex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
char oex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
const int in_str = 1;
short oec = ((idc << 2) + 4 <= chanel) ? 4 : (chanel & 3);
Ti4   val[4];
int   i;
for (i = 0; i < 4; ++i) {
val[i] = 0;
if (iex > 0) {
val[0] = vload4(in_off, in + offset_in);
if (iex > 1) {
val[1] = vload4(in_off + in_str, in + offset_in);
if (iex > 2) {
val[2] = vload4(in_off + (in_str << 1), in + offset_in);
if (iex > 3) {
val[3] = vload4(in_off + in_str * 3, in + offset_in);
int owh_str = width * height;
if (oex == 4) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].x, val[1].x, val[2].x, val[3].x), 0, out + out_off);
if (oec > 1) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].y, val[1].y, val[2].y, val[3].y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str);
if (oec > 2) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].z, val[1].z, val[2].z, val[3].z), 0, out + out_off + (owh_str << 1));
if (oec > 3) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].w, val[1].w, val[2].w, val[3].w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 3);
} else {
if (oex == 1) {
out[out_off] = val[0].x;
if (oec > 1) {
out[out_off + owh_str] = val[0].y;
if (oec > 2) {
out[out_off + (owh_str << 1)] = val[0].z;
if (oec > 3) {
out[out_off + owh_str * 3] = val[0].w;
if (oex == 2) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].x, val[1].x), 0, out + out_off);
if (oec > 1) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].y, val[1].y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str);
if (oec > 2) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].z, val[1].z), 0, out + out_off + (owh_str << 1));
if (oec > 3) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].w, val[1].w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 3);
if (oex == 3) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].x, val[1].x, val[2].x), 0, out + out_off);
if (oec > 1) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].y, val[1].y, val[2].y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str);
if (oec > 2) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].z, val[1].z, val[2].z), 0, out + out_off + (owh_str << 1));
if (oec > 3) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].w, val[1].w, val[2].w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 3);

__kernel void softmax_channel(GLOBAL_SIZE_3_DIMS __global const T* input, __global T* output,
__private const int in_offset, __private const int out_offset,
__private const int output_channels, __private const int remain_channels,
__private const int4 shape)
const int channel_block_idx = get_global_id(0);
const int width_idx         = get_global_id(1);
const int batch_height_idx  = get_global_id(2);
DEAL_NON_UNIFORM_DIM3(channel_block_idx, width_idx, batch_height_idx);
const int batch_idx       = batch_height_idx / shape.z;
const int height_idx      = batch_height_idx % shape.z;
const int offset          = (((batch_idx * shape.y + 0) * shape.z + height_idx) * shape.w + width_idx) * 4;
T         float_max_value = -FLT_MAX;
T4        input_data;
for (short i = 0; i < global_size_dim0 - 1; ++i) {
input_data      = vload4(i * shape.z * shape.w, input + in_offset + offset);
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.x);
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.y);
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.z);
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.w);
input_data = vload4((global_size_dim0 - 1) * shape.z * shape.w, input + in_offset + offset);
if (remain_channels == 0) {
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.w);
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.z);
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.y);
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.x);
} else if (remain_channels == 1) {
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.z);
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.y);
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.x);
} else if (remain_channels == 2) {
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.y);
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.x);
} else if (remain_channels == 3) {
float_max_value = max(float_max_value, input_data.x);
T accum_result = 0;
for (short i = 0; i < global_size_dim0 - 1; ++i) {
input_data = vload4(i * shape.z * shape.w, input + in_offset + offset);
input_data = exp(input_data - float_max_value);
accum_result += input_data.x;
accum_result += input_data.y;
accum_result += input_data.z;
accum_result += input_data.w;
input_data = vload4((global_size_dim0 - 1) * shape.z * shape.w, input + in_offset + offset);
input_data -= float_max_value;
if (remain_channels == 0) {
accum_result += exp(input_data.w);
accum_result += exp(input_data.z);
accum_result += exp(input_data.y);
accum_result += exp(input_data.x);
} else if (remain_channels == 1) {
accum_result += exp(input_data.z);
accum_result += exp(input_data.y);
accum_result += exp(input_data.x);
} else if (remain_channels == 2) {
accum_result += exp(input_data.y);
accum_result += exp(input_data.x);
} else if (remain_channels == 3) {
accum_result += exp(input_data.x);
input_data              = vload4(channel_block_idx * shape.z * shape.w, input + in_offset + offset) - float_max_value;
const int output_remain = output_channels - mul24(channel_block_idx, 4);
if (output_remain == 1) {
input_data.x = exp(input_data.x) / accum_result;
} else if (output_remain == 2) {
input_data.y = exp(input_data.y) / accum_result;
input_data.x = exp(input_data.x) / accum_result;
} else if (output_remain == 3) {
input_data.z = exp(input_data.z) / accum_result;
input_data.y = exp(input_data.y) / accum_result;
input_data.x = exp(input_data.x) / accum_result;
} else {
input_data = exp(input_data) / accum_result;
vstore4(input_data, channel_block_idx * shape.z * shape.w, output + out_offset + offset);
__kernel void softmax_height(__global const T* input, __global T* output, __private const int in_offset,
__private const int  out_offset,
__private const int4 shape)
int wc = get_global_id(0);
int b  = get_global_id(1);
const int c      = wc / shape.w;
const int w      = wc % shape.w;
const int offset = (((b * shape.y + c) * shape.z + 0) * shape.w + w) * 4;
if (wc < shape.y * shape.w && b < shape.x) {
T4 maxValue = vload4(0, input + in_offset + offset);
for (int i = 1; i < shape.z; ++i) {
maxValue = fmax(maxValue, vload4(i * shape.w, input + in_offset + offset));
T4 sumValue = (T4)0;
for (int i = 0; i < shape.z; ++i) {
sumValue += exp(vload4(i * shape.w, input + in_offset + offset) - maxValue);
for (int i = 0; i < shape.z; ++i) {
T4 value = exp(vload4(i * shape.w, input + in_offset + offset) - maxValue) / sumValue;
vstore4(value, i * shape.w, output + out_offset + offset);
__kernel void softmax_width(__global const T* input, __global T* output, __private const int in_offset,
__private const int  out_offset,
__private const int4 shape)
int c  = get_global_id(0);
int bh = get_global_id(1);
const int b      = bh / shape.z;
const int h      = bh % shape.z;
const int offset = (((b * shape.y + c) * shape.z + h) * shape.w + 0) * 4;
if (c < shape.y && bh < shape.x * shape.z) {
T4 maxValue = vload4(0, input + in_offset + offset);
for (int i = 1; i < shape.w; ++i) {
maxValue = fmax(maxValue, vload4(i, input + in_offset + offset));
T4 sumValue = (T4)0;
for (int i = 0; i < shape.w; ++i) {
sumValue += exp(vload4(i, input + in_offset + offset) - maxValue);
for (int i = 0; i < shape.w; ++i) {
T4 value = exp(vload4(i, input + in_offset + offset) - maxValue) / sumValue;
vstore4(value, i, output + out_offset + offset);

__kernel void transpose_nchw(__global const T* in, __global T* out, const int iw_str, const int ih_str,
const int ow_str, const int oh_str, const int dim0, const int dim1, const int dim2,
const int iw, const int in_offset, const int out_offset)
int idx = get_global_id(0);
int idy = get_global_id(1);
int idz = get_global_id(2);
if (idx >= (iw + 3) / 4 || idy >= ih_str) {
return;
char      ew     = (((idx << 2) + 4) <= iw) ? 4 : (iw & 3);
T4        val    = 0;
const int in_off = (idz * ih_str + idy) * iw_str + (idx << 2) + in_offset;
if (ew == 4) {
val = vload4(0, in + in_off);
} else {
if (ew == 1) {
val.x = in[in_off];
if (ew == 2) {
val.xy = vload2(0, in + in_off);
if (ew == 3) {
val.xyz = vload3(0, in + in_off);
int ox      = idx << 2;
int oy      = idy;
int oz      = idz;
int out_str = 1;
if (dim0 == 1) {
oz = idy;
if (dim0 == 2) {
oz      = idx << 2;
out_str = ow_str * oh_str;
if (dim1 == 0) {
oy = idz;
if (dim1 == 2) {
oy      = idx << 2;
out_str = ow_str;
if (dim2 == 0) {
ox = idz;
if (dim2 == 1) {
ox = idy;
int out_off  = (oz * oh_str + oy) * ow_str + ox + out_offset;
out[out_off] = val.x;
if (ew > 1) {
out[out_off + out_str] = val.y;
if (ew > 2) {
out[out_off + out_str * 2] = val.z;
if (ew > 3) {
out[out_off + out_str * 3] = val.w;

#define T8 half8

return 1.0h / (1.0h + native_exp(-x));
static T4 sigmoid_f_v4(T4 x)
return (T4)1.0h / ( (T4)1.0h + exp(-x));

__kernel void debug_printFloat16Buffer(__global const T *input, const int in_offset)
const ushort idx_batch = get_global_id(0);
const ushort idx_hidden = get_global_id(1);

__kernel void gru_multi_seq_forward(
__global const T *in_buf,
__global const T *in_buf_weight_ih,
__global const T *in_buf_weight_hh,
__global const T *in_buf_bias,
__global T *in_buf_hidden,
#if HAS_TWO_OUTPUTS
__global T *out_buf_all_hiddens,
__global T *out_buf_last_hidden,
#else
#if LAST_OUT_HIDDEN
__global T *out_buf_last_hidden,
#else
__global T *out_buf_all_hiddens,
#endif
#endif
__private const int in_buf_offset,
__private const int weight_ih_offset,
__private const int weight_hh_offset,
__private const int bias_buf_offset,
__private const int seq_size,
__private const int in_hidden_offset,
#if HAS_TWO_OUTPUTS
__private const int out_buf_offset,
__private const int out_hidden_offset,
#else
#if LAST_OUT_HIDDEN
__private const int out_hidden_offset,
#else
__private const int out_buf_offset,
#endif
#endif
__private const int direction,
__private const int hidden_size,
__private const int batch_size,
__private const int seq_length,
__private const int input_size
const ushort idx_batch = get_global_id(0);
ushort idx_hidden = get_global_id(1) * 4;
__global const T *input = in_buf + in_buf_offset;
__global const T *in_weight_ih = in_buf_weight_ih + weight_ih_offset;
__global const T *in_weight_hh = in_buf_weight_hh + weight_hh_offset;
__global const T *in_bias =  in_buf_bias + bias_buf_offset;
__global const T *h_prev = in_buf_hidden + in_hidden_offset;
#if HAS_TWO_OUTPUTS
__global  T *out_last_hidden =  out_buf_last_hidden + out_hidden_offset;
__global  T *out_all_hiddens =  out_buf_all_hiddens + out_buf_offset;
#else
#if LAST_OUT_HIDDEN
__global  T *out_last_hidden = out_buf_last_hidden + out_hidden_offset;
#else
__global  T *out_all_hiddens = out_buf_all_hiddens + out_buf_offset;
#endif
#endif
const ushort in_offset = batch_size * input_size;
const ushort out_offset = batch_size * hidden_size;
const ushort init_hi_idx = idx_batch * hidden_size;
const ushort bias_offset = 3*hidden_size;
T4 tmp_out = (T4)0.0h;
for (ushort t = 0; t < seq_length; t++) {
ushort ti = (direction==1) ? seq_length - 1 - t : t;
ushort x_t_idx = ti * in_offset + idx_batch * input_size;
ushort out_idx = ti * out_offset + idx_batch * hidden_size + idx_hidden;
T4 z_t = (T4)0.0h;
T4 r_t = (T4)0.0h;
T4 h_candidate_t = (T4)0.0h;
T4 tmp_n = (T4)0.0h;
T4 _in_w_r =  (T4)0.0h;
T4 _in_w_z =  (T4)0.0h;
T4 _in_w_n =  (T4)0.0h;
T4 _in_data = (T4)0.0h;
T4 _in_bias_r = (T4)0.0h;
T4 _in_bias_z = (T4)0.0h;
T4 _in_bias_n = (T4)0.0h;
const ushort comp_p_sz = 4;
for (ushort i = 0; i < input_size; i+=comp_p_sz) {
_in_w_z = vload4(0, in_weight_ih + (i*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden));
_in_w_r = vload4(0, in_weight_ih + (i*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + hidden_size));
_in_w_n = vload4(0, in_weight_ih + (i*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + 2*hidden_size));
_in_data = vload4(0, input + (x_t_idx + i));
z_t = mad(_in_w_z, _in_data.s0, z_t);
r_t = mad(_in_w_r, _in_data.s0, r_t);
h_candidate_t = mad(_in_w_n, _in_data.s0, h_candidate_t);
_in_w_z = vload4(0, in_weight_ih + ((i+1)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden));
_in_w_r = vload4(0, in_weight_ih + ((i+1)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + hidden_size));
_in_w_n = vload4(0, in_weight_ih + ((i+1)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + 2*hidden_size));
z_t = mad(_in_w_z, _in_data.s1, z_t);
r_t = mad(_in_w_r, _in_data.s1, r_t);
h_candidate_t = mad(_in_w_n, _in_data.s1, h_candidate_t);
_in_w_z = vload4(0, in_weight_ih + ((i+2)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden));
_in_w_r = vload4(0, in_weight_ih + ((i+2)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + hidden_size));
_in_w_n = vload4(0, in_weight_ih + ((i+2)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + 2*hidden_size));
z_t = mad(_in_w_z, _in_data.s2, z_t);
r_t = mad(_in_w_r, _in_data.s2, r_t);
h_candidate_t = mad(_in_w_n, _in_data.s2, h_candidate_t);
_in_w_z = vload4(0, in_weight_ih + ((i+3)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden));
_in_w_r = vload4(0, in_weight_ih + ((i+3)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + hidden_size));
_in_w_n = vload4(0, in_weight_ih + ((i+3)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + 2*hidden_size));
z_t = mad(_in_w_z, _in_data.s3, z_t);
r_t = mad(_in_w_r, _in_data.s3, r_t);
h_candidate_t = mad(_in_w_n, _in_data.s3, h_candidate_t);
for (ushort i = 0; i < hidden_size; i+=comp_p_sz) {
_in_w_z = vload4(0, in_weight_hh + (i*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden));
_in_w_r = vload4(0, in_weight_hh + (i*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + hidden_size));
_in_w_n = vload4(0, in_weight_hh + (i*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + 2*hidden_size));
_in_data = vload4(0, h_prev + (init_hi_idx+i));
z_t = mad(_in_w_z, _in_data.s0, z_t);
r_t = mad(_in_w_r, _in_data.s0, r_t);
tmp_n = mad(_in_w_n, _in_data.s0, tmp_n);
_in_w_z = vload4(0, in_weight_hh + ((i+1)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden));
_in_w_r = vload4(0, in_weight_hh + ((i+1)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + hidden_size));
_in_w_n = vload4(0, in_weight_hh + ((i+1)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + 2*hidden_size));
z_t = mad(_in_w_z, _in_data.s1, z_t);
r_t = mad(_in_w_r, _in_data.s1, r_t);
tmp_n = mad(_in_w_n, _in_data.s1, tmp_n);
_in_w_z = vload4(0, in_weight_hh + ((i+2)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden));
_in_w_r = vload4(0, in_weight_hh + ((i+2)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + hidden_size));
_in_w_n = vload4(0, in_weight_hh + ((i+2)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + 2*hidden_size));
z_t = mad(_in_w_z, _in_data.s2, z_t);
r_t = mad(_in_w_r, _in_data.s2, r_t);
tmp_n = mad(_in_w_n, _in_data.s2, tmp_n);
_in_w_z = vload4(0, in_weight_hh + ((i+3)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden));
_in_w_r = vload4(0, in_weight_hh + ((i+3)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + hidden_size));
_in_w_n = vload4(0, in_weight_hh + ((i+3)*3*hidden_size + idx_hidden + 2*hidden_size));
z_t = mad(_in_w_z, _in_data.s3, z_t);
r_t = mad(_in_w_r, _in_data.s3, r_t);
tmp_n = mad(_in_w_n, _in_data.s3, tmp_n);
_in_bias_z = vload4(0, in_bias + (idx_hidden));
_in_bias_r = vload4(0, in_bias + (1*hidden_size+idx_hidden));
_in_bias_n = vload4(0, in_bias + (2*hidden_size+idx_hidden));
z_t += _in_bias_z;
r_t += _in_bias_r;
h_candidate_t += _in_bias_n;
_in_bias_z = vload4(0, in_bias + bias_offset + (idx_hidden));
_in_bias_r = vload4(0, in_bias + bias_offset + (1*hidden_size+idx_hidden));
_in_bias_n = vload4(0, in_bias + bias_offset + (2*hidden_size+idx_hidden));
z_t += _in_bias_z;
r_t += _in_bias_r;
tmp_n += _in_bias_n;
r_t = sigmoid_f_v4(r_t);
z_t = sigmoid_f_v4(z_t);
h_candidate_t = tanh(mad(tmp_n, r_t, h_candidate_t));
_in_data = vload4(0, h_prev + (init_hi_idx + idx_hidden));
tmp_out = z_t*_in_data;
tmp_out += mad(z_t, -1.0h*h_candidate_t , h_candidate_t);
if (seq_length > 1) {
vstore4(tmp_out.s0123, 0, h_prev + (init_hi_idx + idx_hidden));
barrier(CLK_LOCAL_MEM_FENCE);
#if HAS_TWO_OUTPUTS || !LAST_OUT_HIDDEN
vstore4(tmp_out.s0123, 0, out_all_hiddens + out_idx);
#endif
#if HAS_TWO_OUTPUTS || LAST_OUT_HIDDEN
vstore4(tmp_out.s0123, 0, out_last_hidden + (init_hi_idx + idx_hidden));
#endif
}#define SUPPORT_FP16
#ifdef SUPPORT_FP16
#pragma OPENCL EXTENSION cl_khr_fp16 : enable
#define T half
#define T4 half4
#define T8 half8
#define T16 half16
static T sigmoid_f(T x)
return 1.0h / (1.0h + native_exp(-x));
static T4 sigmoid_f_v4(T4 x)
return (T4)1.0h / ( (T4)1.0h + exp(-x));
static T8 sigmoid_f_v8(T8 x)
return (T8)1.0h / ( (T8)1.0h + exp(-x));
#endif
#pragma OPENCL EXTENSION cl_arm_printf : enable
__kernel void gru_input_transform(
__global const T *in_buf,
__global const T *in_buf_weight_ih,
__global const T *in_buf_bias,
__global T *output_gates,
__private const int in_buf_offset,
__private const int weight_ih_offset,
__private const int bias_buf_offset,
__private const int input_size,
__private const int hidden_size,
__private const int num_dir)
const int seq_batch_idx = get_global_id(0);
const int dir_hid_idx = get_global_id(1) * 8;
const uint hid_idx = dir_hid_idx % (3*hidden_size);
uint direction = dir_hid_idx / (3*hidden_size);
__global const T *input = in_buf + in_buf_offset;
__global const T *in_weight_ih = in_buf_weight_ih + weight_ih_offset ;
__global const T *in_bias = in_buf_bias + bias_buf_offset;
T8 tmp_out = (T8)0.0h;
T8 _in_w = (T8)0.0h;
T4 _in_data = (T4)0.0h;
const uint in_offset = seq_batch_idx * input_size;
const uint w_fw_bw_offset = direction*3*hidden_size*input_size;
const uint b_fw_bw_offset = direction*6*hidden_size;
tmp_out = vload8(0, in_bias + b_fw_bw_offset + hid_idx);
for (int i = 0; i < input_size; i+=4) {
_in_data = vload4(0, input + in_offset + i);
_in_w = vload8(0, in_weight_ih + (i*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_idx));
tmp_out = mad(_in_data.s0, _in_w, tmp_out);
_in_w = vload8(0, in_weight_ih + ((i+1)*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_idx));
tmp_out = mad(_in_data.s1, _in_w, tmp_out);
_in_w = vload8(0, in_weight_ih + ((i+2)*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset+ hid_idx));
tmp_out = mad(_in_data.s2, _in_w, tmp_out);
_in_w = vload8(0, in_weight_ih + ((i+3)*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_idx));
tmp_out = mad(_in_data.s3, _in_w, tmp_out);
const uint out_offset = (num_dir == 1)? seq_batch_idx*3*hidden_size + dir_hid_idx :
seq_batch_idx*6*hidden_size + dir_hid_idx;
vstore8(tmp_out, 0, output_gates + out_offset);
__kernel void gru_hidden_compute(
__global const T* interim_input,
__global const T* in_buf_weight_hh,
__global const T* in_buf_bias,
__global T *in_buf_hidden,
#if HAS_TWO_OUTPUTS
__global T *out_buf_all_hiddens,
__global T *out_buf_last_hidden,
#else
#if LAST_OUT_HIDDEN
__global T *out_buf_last_hidden,
#else
__global T *out_buf_all_hiddens,
#endif
#endif
__private const int in_hidden_offset,
#if HAS_TWO_OUTPUTS
__private const int out_buf_offset,
__private const int out_hidden_offset,
#else
#if LAST_OUT_HIDDEN
__private const int out_hidden_offset,
#else
__private const int out_buf_offset,
#endif
#endif
__private const int seq_idx,
__global T *tmp_hidden_buf,
__private const int weight_hh_offset,
__private const int bias_buf_offset,
__private const int batch_size,
__private const int hidden_size,
__private const int seq_length,
__private const int num_dir,
__private const uchar reset_hid_buf)
const uint batch_id = get_global_id(0);
const uint hid_dir_id = get_global_id(1) * 4 ;
const uint hid_id = hid_dir_id % hidden_size;
__global const T *weight_hh = in_buf_weight_hh + weight_hh_offset;
__global const T *bias_hh = in_buf_bias + bias_buf_offset;
__global  T* h_prev = in_buf_hidden + in_hidden_offset;
#if HAS_TWO_OUTPUTS
__global  T *out_last_hidden =  out_buf_last_hidden + out_hidden_offset;
__global  T *out_all_hiddens =  out_buf_all_hiddens + out_buf_offset;
#else
#if LAST_OUT_HIDDEN
__global  T *out_last_hidden = out_buf_last_hidden + out_hidden_offset;
#else
__global  T *out_all_hiddens = out_buf_all_hiddens + out_buf_offset;
#endif
#endif
T4 z_gate = (T4)0.0h;
T4 r_gate = (T4)0.0h;
T4 n_gate = (T4)0.0h;
T4 h_candidate_gate = (T4)0.0h;
T4 w_r =  (T4)0.0h;
T4 w_z =  (T4)0.0h;
T4 w_n =  (T4)0.0h;
T4 tmp_out = (T4)0.0h;
T4 in_hi_data = (T4)0.0h;
const uint direction = hid_dir_id / hidden_size;
const uint batch_hid_sz = batch_size * hidden_size;
const uint init_hi_idx = (num_dir == 1)? batch_id * hidden_size :
direction * batch_hid_sz + batch_id * hidden_size;
const uint bias_offset = (num_dir == 1)? 3*hidden_size : direction*6*hidden_size + 3*hidden_size;
const uint out_dir_idx = (direction==0)? seq_idx : seq_length - seq_idx;
const uint seq_batch_idx = out_dir_idx * batch_size + batch_id;
const uint out_part_idx =  direction * batch_hid_sz + batch_id * hidden_size + hid_id;
uint out_idx = (num_dir == 1)? seq_idx * batch_hid_sz + batch_id * hidden_size + hid_id :
seq_idx * num_dir * batch_hid_sz + out_part_idx;
if (direction==1 && num_dir == 2)
out_idx = out_dir_idx * num_dir * batch_hid_sz + out_part_idx;
const uint gate_offset = (num_dir == 1)? seq_batch_idx * 3*hidden_size :
seq_batch_idx*6*hidden_size + direction*3*hidden_size;
const uint w_fw_bw_offset = direction*3*hidden_size*hidden_size;
__global T *init_hid_buf = ((seq_idx % 2) == 0)? h_prev : tmp_hidden_buf;
for (ushort i = 0; i < hidden_size; i+=4) {
in_hi_data = vload4(0, init_hid_buf + (init_hi_idx + i));
w_z = vload4(0, weight_hh + (i*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_id));
w_r = vload4(0, weight_hh + (i*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_id + hidden_size));
w_n = vload4(0, weight_hh + (i*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_id + 2*hidden_size));
z_gate = mad(w_z, in_hi_data.s0, z_gate);
r_gate = mad(w_r, in_hi_data.s0, r_gate);
n_gate = mad(w_n, in_hi_data.s0, n_gate);
w_z = vload4(0, weight_hh + ((i+1)*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_id));
w_r = vload4(0, weight_hh + ((i+1)*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_id + hidden_size));
w_n = vload4(0, weight_hh + ((i+1)*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_id + 2*hidden_size));
z_gate = mad(w_z, in_hi_data.s1, z_gate);
r_gate = mad(w_r, in_hi_data.s1, r_gate);
n_gate = mad(w_n, in_hi_data.s1, n_gate);
w_z = vload4(0, weight_hh + ((i+2)*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_id));
w_r = vload4(0, weight_hh + ((i+2)*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_id + hidden_size));
w_n = vload4(0, weight_hh + ((i+2)*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_id + 2*hidden_size));
z_gate = mad(w_z, in_hi_data.s2, z_gate);
r_gate = mad(w_r, in_hi_data.s2, r_gate);
n_gate = mad(w_n, in_hi_data.s2, n_gate);
w_z = vload4(0, weight_hh + ((i+3)*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_id));
w_r = vload4(0, weight_hh + ((i+3)*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_id + hidden_size));
w_n = vload4(0, weight_hh + ((i+3)*3*hidden_size + w_fw_bw_offset + hid_id + 2*hidden_size));
z_gate = mad(w_z, in_hi_data.s3, z_gate);
r_gate = mad(w_r, in_hi_data.s3, r_gate);
n_gate = mad(w_n, in_hi_data.s3, n_gate);
z_gate += vload4(0, interim_input + (gate_offset + hid_id) );
r_gate += vload4(0, interim_input + (gate_offset + hidden_size + hid_id) );
h_candidate_gate = vload4(0, interim_input + (gate_offset + 2*hidden_size + hid_id) );
T4 bias_z = vload4(0, bias_hh + bias_offset + hid_id);
T4 bias_r = vload4(0, bias_hh + bias_offset + hidden_size + hid_id);
T4 bias_n = vload4(0, bias_hh + bias_offset + 2*hidden_size + hid_id);
z_gate += bias_z;
r_gate += bias_r;
n_gate += bias_n;
z_gate = sigmoid_f_v4(z_gate);
r_gate = sigmoid_f_v4(r_gate);
h_candidate_gate = tanh(mad(n_gate, r_gate, h_candidate_gate) );
T4 tmp_in_hi_data = vload4(0, init_hid_buf + (init_hi_idx + hid_id));
tmp_out = z_gate * tmp_in_hi_data;
tmp_out += mad(z_gate, -1.0h*h_candidate_gate , h_candidate_gate);
if (seq_idx < seq_length ) {
__global T *tmp_out_hid_buf = ((seq_idx % 2) == 0)? tmp_hidden_buf : h_prev;
vstore4(tmp_out, 0, tmp_out_hid_buf + (init_hi_idx + hid_id));
else if (seq_idx == seq_length) {
if (reset_hid_buf)
vstore4((T4)(0.0h), 0, h_prev + (init_hi_idx + hid_id));
#if HAS_TWO_OUTPUTS || !LAST_OUT_HIDDEN
vstore4(tmp_out, 0, out_all_hiddens + out_idx);
#endif
#if HAS_TWO_OUTPUTS || LAST_OUT_HIDDEN
if (seq_idx == seq_length)
vstore4(tmp_out, 0, out_last_hidden + (init_hi_idx + hid_id));
#endif
}#pragma OPENCL EXTENSION cl_khr_fp16 : enable
__kernel void unpack_nchwc8_to_nchw(__global Ti* in, __global To* out, const int align_wh, const int width,
const int height, const int chanel, const int offset_in, const int offset_out,
int zp, float scale, int batch, int in_batch_offset, int out_batch_offset)
const int idh  = get_global_id(0);
const int idw  = get_global_id(1);
const int idnc = get_global_id(2);
int idc      = idnc / batch;
int batch_id = idnc % batch;
if ((idw >= ((width + 3) >> 2)) || idh >= height || (idc >= ((chanel + 7) >> 3))) {
return;
int  in_off  = idc * align_wh + idh * width + (idw << 2) + batch_id * in_batch_offset;
int  out_off = ((idc << 3) * height + idh) * width + (idw << 2) + offset_out + batch_id * out_batch_offset;
char iex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
char oex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
const int in_str = 1;
short oec = ((idc << 3) + 8 <= chanel) ? 8 : (chanel & 7);
Ti8 val[4];
int i;
for (i = 0; i < 4; ++i) {
val[i] = 0;
if (iex > 0) {
val[0] = vload8(in_off, in + offset_in);
if (iex > 1) {
val[1] = vload8(in_off + in_str, in + offset_in);
if (iex > 2) {
val[2] = vload8(in_off + (in_str << 1), in + offset_in);
if (iex > 3) {
val[3] = vload8(in_off + in_str * 3, in + offset_in);
int owh_str = width * height;
if (oex == 4) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].lo.x, val[1].lo.x, val[2].lo.x, val[3].lo.x), 0, out + out_off);
if (oec > 1) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].lo.y, val[1].lo.y, val[2].lo.y, val[3].lo.y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str);
if (oec > 2) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].lo.z, val[1].lo.z, val[2].lo.z, val[3].lo.z), 0, out + out_off + (owh_str << 1));
if (oec > 3) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].lo.w, val[1].lo.w, val[2].lo.w, val[3].lo.w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 3);
if (oec > 4) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].hi.x, val[1].hi.x, val[2].hi.x, val[3].hi.x), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 4);
if (oec > 5) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].hi.y, val[1].hi.y, val[2].hi.y, val[3].hi.y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 5);
if (oec > 6) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].hi.z, val[1].hi.z, val[2].hi.z, val[3].hi.z), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 6);
if (oec > 7) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].hi.w, val[1].hi.w, val[2].hi.w, val[3].hi.w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 7);
} else {
if (oex == 1) {
out[out_off] = val[0].lo.x;
if (oec > 1) {
out[out_off + owh_str] = val[0].lo.y;
if (oec > 2) {
out[out_off + (owh_str << 1)] = val[0].lo.z;
if (oec > 3) {
out[out_off + owh_str * 3] = val[0].lo.w;
if (oec > 4) {
out[out_off + owh_str * 4] = val[0].hi.x;
if (oec > 5) {
out[out_off + owh_str * 5] = val[0].hi.y;
if (oec > 6) {
out[out_off + owh_str * 6] = val[0].hi.z;
if (oec > 7) {
out[out_off + owh_str * 7] = val[0].hi.w;
if (oex == 2) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].lo.x, val[1].lo.x), 0, out + out_off);
if (oec > 1) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].lo.y, val[1].lo.y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str);
if (oec > 2) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].lo.z, val[1].lo.z), 0, out + out_off + (owh_str << 1));
if (oec > 3) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].lo.w, val[1].lo.w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 3);
if (oec > 4) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].hi.x, val[1].hi.x), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 4);
if (oec > 5) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].hi.y, val[1].hi.y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 5);
if (oec > 6) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].hi.z, val[1].hi.z), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 6);
if (oec > 7) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].hi.w, val[1].hi.w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 7);
if (oex == 3) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].lo.x, val[1].lo.x, val[2].lo.x), 0, out + out_off);
if (oec > 1) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].lo.y, val[1].lo.y, val[2].lo.y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str);
if (oec > 2) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].lo.z, val[1].lo.z, val[2].lo.z), 0, out + out_off + (owh_str << 1));
if (oec > 3) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].lo.w, val[1].lo.w, val[2].lo.w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 3);
if (oec > 4) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].hi.x, val[1].hi.x, val[2].hi.x), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 4);
if (oec > 5) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].hi.y, val[1].hi.y, val[2].hi.y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 5);
if (oec > 6) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].hi.z, val[1].hi.z, val[2].hi.z), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 6);
if (oec > 7) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].hi.w, val[1].hi.w, val[2].hi.w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 7);
__kernel void unpack_nchwc8_to_nchw_dequant(__global Ti* in, __global To* out, const int align_wh, const int width,
const int height, const int chanel, const int offset_in,
const int offset_out, int zp, float scale)
const int idh = get_global_id(0);
const int idw = get_global_id(1);
const int idc = get_global_id(2);
if ((idw >= ((width + 3) >> 2)) || idh >= height || (idc >= ((chanel + 7) >> 3))) {
return;
int  in_off  = idc * align_wh + idh * width + (idw << 2);
int  out_off = ((idc << 3) * height + idh) * width + (idw << 2) + offset_out;
char iex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
char oex     = ((idw << 2) + 4 <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
const int in_str = 1;
short oec = ((idc << 3) + 8 <= chanel) ? 8 : (chanel & 7);
Ti8   ival;
To8 val[4];
int i;
for (i = 0; i < 4; ++i) {
val[i] = 0;
if (iex > 0) {
ival = vload8(in_off, in + offset_in);
val[0] =
(To8)((ival.lo.x - zp) * scale, (ival.lo.y - zp) * scale, (ival.lo.z - zp) * scale, (ival.lo.w - zp) * scale,
(ival.hi.x - zp) * scale, (ival.hi.y - zp) * scale, (ival.hi.z - zp) * scale, (ival.hi.w - zp) * scale);
if (iex > 1) {
ival = vload8(in_off + in_str, in + offset_in);
val[1] =
(To8)((ival.lo.x - zp) * scale, (ival.lo.y - zp) * scale, (ival.lo.z - zp) * scale, (ival.lo.w - zp) * scale,
(ival.hi.x - zp) * scale, (ival.hi.y - zp) * scale, (ival.hi.z - zp) * scale, (ival.hi.w - zp) * scale);
if (iex > 2) {
ival = vload8(in_off + (in_str << 1), in + offset_in);
val[2] =
(To8)((ival.lo.x - zp) * scale, (ival.lo.y - zp) * scale, (ival.lo.z - zp) * scale, (ival.lo.w - zp) * scale,
(ival.hi.x - zp) * scale, (ival.hi.y - zp) * scale, (ival.hi.z - zp) * scale, (ival.hi.w - zp) * scale);
if (iex > 3) {
ival = vload8(in_off + in_str * 3, in + offset_in);
val[3] =
(To8)((ival.lo.x - zp) * scale, (ival.lo.y - zp) * scale, (ival.lo.z - zp) * scale, (ival.lo.w - zp) * scale,
(ival.hi.x - zp) * scale, (ival.hi.y - zp) * scale, (ival.hi.z - zp) * scale, (ival.hi.w - zp) * scale);
int owh_str = width * height;
if (oex == 4) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].lo.x, val[1].lo.x, val[2].lo.x, val[3].lo.x), 0, out + out_off);
if (oec > 1) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].lo.y, val[1].lo.y, val[2].lo.y, val[3].lo.y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str);
if (oec > 2) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].lo.z, val[1].lo.z, val[2].lo.z, val[3].lo.z), 0, out + out_off + (owh_str << 1));
if (oec > 3) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].lo.w, val[1].lo.w, val[2].lo.w, val[3].lo.w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 3);
if (oec > 4) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].hi.x, val[1].hi.x, val[2].hi.x, val[3].hi.x), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 4);
if (oec > 5) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].hi.y, val[1].hi.y, val[2].hi.y, val[3].hi.y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 5);
if (oec > 6) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].hi.z, val[1].hi.z, val[2].hi.z, val[3].hi.z), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 6);
if (oec > 7) {
vstore4((To4)(val[0].hi.w, val[1].hi.w, val[2].hi.w, val[3].hi.w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 7);
} else {
if (oex == 1) {
out[out_off] = val[0].lo.x;
if (oec > 1) {
out[out_off + owh_str] = val[0].lo.y;
if (oec > 2) {
out[out_off + (owh_str << 1)] = val[0].lo.z;
if (oec > 3) {
out[out_off + owh_str * 3] = val[0].lo.w;
if (oec > 4) {
out[out_off + owh_str * 4] = val[0].hi.x;
if (oec > 5) {
out[out_off + owh_str * 5] = val[0].hi.y;
if (oec > 6) {
out[out_off + owh_str * 6] = val[0].hi.z;
if (oec > 7) {
out[out_off + owh_str * 7] = val[0].hi.w;
if (oex == 2) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].lo.x, val[1].lo.x), 0, out + out_off);
if (oec > 1) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].lo.y, val[1].lo.y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str);
if (oec > 2) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].lo.z, val[1].lo.z), 0, out + out_off + (owh_str << 1));
if (oec > 3) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].lo.w, val[1].lo.w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 3);
if (oec > 4) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].hi.x, val[1].hi.x), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 4);
if (oec > 5) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].hi.y, val[1].hi.y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 5);
if (oec > 6) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].hi.z, val[1].hi.z), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 6);
if (oec > 7) {
vstore2((To2)(val[0].hi.w, val[1].hi.w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 7);
if (oex == 3) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].lo.x, val[1].lo.x, val[2].lo.x), 0, out + out_off);
if (oec > 1) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].lo.y, val[1].lo.y, val[2].lo.y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str);
if (oec > 2) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].lo.z, val[1].lo.z, val[2].lo.z), 0, out + out_off + (owh_str << 1));
if (oec > 3) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].lo.w, val[1].lo.w, val[2].lo.w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 3);
if (oec > 4) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].hi.x, val[1].hi.x, val[2].hi.x), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 4);
if (oec > 5) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].hi.y, val[1].hi.y, val[2].hi.y), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 5);
if (oec > 6) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].hi.z, val[1].hi.z, val[2].hi.z), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 6);
if (oec > 7) {
vstore3((To3)(val[0].hi.w, val[1].hi.w, val[2].hi.w), 0, out + out_off + owh_str * 7);

__kernel void convert_nchw_to_nchw(__global Ti* in, __global To* out, const int width_stride, const int width,
const int height, const int chanel, const int offset_in, const int offset_out)
const int idh = get_global_id(0);
const int idw = get_global_id(1);
const int idc = get_global_id(2);
if (idw >= ((width + 3) >> 2) || idh >= height) {
return;
char ie = (((idw << 2) + 4) <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
char oe = (((idw << 2) + 4) <= width) ? 4 : (width & 3);
if (idw >= ((width + 3) >> 2) || idh >= height || idc >= chanel) {
ie = 0;
Ti4        val    = 0;
const int in_off = (idc * height + idh) * width + (idw << 2) + offset_in;
if (ie == 4) {
val = vload4(0, in + in_off);
} else {
if (ie == 1) {
val.x = in[in_off];
if (ie == 2) {
T2 tmp = vload2(0, in + in_off);
val.x  = tmp.x;
val.y  = tmp.y;
if (ie == 3) {
T3 tmp = vload3(0, in + in_off);
val.x  = tmp.x;
val.y  = tmp.y;
val.z  = tmp.z;
To4 val_o = CONVERT(val);
const int out_off = (idc * height + idh) * width + (idw << 2) + offset_out;
if (oe == 4) {
vstore4(val_o, 0, out + out_off);
} else {
if (oe == 1) {
out[out_off] = val_o.x;
if (oe == 2) {
vstore2(val_o.xy, 0, out + out_off);
if (oe == 3) {
vstore3(val_o.xyz, 0, out + out_off);
